eldest highte algarsyf othir sone clepid camballo doughter hadde worthy kyng also yongest highte canace forto telle hir beaute lith tunge ne connyng dar take high thinge also myn english eke insufficient muste clerk rethour excellent knewe colour longing art sholde discrye hir euery part suche muste speke fyl cambuscan hath twenty wynter bore dyademe wente fro yeer yeer deme leet feste natiuite done crye thorow saray cyte laste idus marche aftir yeer phebus sonne ful ioly cleer exaltacion marti face mansion aries hote colerik signe ful lusty wethir benigne whiche foulis ayens sonne sh • ne seson yonge grene wel loude song affection hem semyd getyn ayen protectiouns agayn swerd wynter kene cold kyng whiche told ryal vestimentis sat deys dyademe ful high paleys holdith feste solempne riche worlde ther non liche whiche yf sholde telle al ray wolde occupye someris day eke nedith deuyse euery cours ordre seruise wol telle strange sewis ne swannys ne heronsewis eke lond tellen knyghtis olde sum mete ful deynte holde lond men recke smal ther noman may reporten al wol tarye pryme fruyt los tyme vnto firste tale wol haue recours befil aftir thridde cours whyle kyng sat high nobleye herkenyng mynstrallis thing pleye beforn hym bord deliciously atte halle dore sodeynly ther cam knyght vpon stede bra hond brood myrrour glas thombe hadde gold ryng side nakid swerd hanging vp ridith high borde al halle ne ther spoke word meruayll knyght hym holde bisely wayten yonge olde straunge knyght cam sodenly al armed saue hed ful richely saluyd kyng quene lordis alle ordre sitten halle high reuerence obeisaunce wel speche contenaunce gawen olde curtesie though com aye • n feirye ne coude hym amende worde aftir high lord manly voys sayde message aftir fourme vsed langage withoute faylle sillabyl lettir tale sholde seme bettir accordyng word chere techith art speche hem lere al sowne styl ne clymbe high hille say thus comyn • ntent thus muche amountith ment haue mynde sayde kyng arabye ynde liege lord solempne day saleweth yow best may sendith honour feste al redy heste stede bra esely wel space day naturel say xxiiij houri liste drougthe showris bere body euery place whiche herte willith forto pase withoute wem thorough foul fair yf list fle high ayer doth egil whan hym list sore stede shal bere euermore withoute harm til ye ye list though ye slepe ba • reste turne ayeen wringyng pyn wroughte knoweth many gyn waytid many constellacion hadde wrought operacion knew meny skyl meny abonde myrrour eke haue myn hond hath suche myght men may se ther shal falle ony aduersite vnto regne vnto self also openly frend foo ouer al ony lady bright hath set herte ony maner wight fals shal treson se newe loue al subtilite openly ther shal thing hyde wherfore agayns lusty someris tyde myrrour ring ye may se sente hath lady canace excellent doughter vertu ring yf ye wol yf list forto vp thombe purs bere foul fleeth vnder heuyn ne shal vnderstonde steuyn knowe menyng openly playn answere hym langage agayn euery gras growith vpon rote shal knowe wol bote al wounde neuer deep wyde nakid swerd hangith side suche vertu hath man ye smyte thorow armure wol kerue byte thicke braunchid ook man woundith strook shal neuer hool til ye list grace stroke hym plat place hurt mykyl sayn ye moot plat swerd agayn stroke hem wounde wol close verray soth withouten glose fayleth whylis holde knyght hath thus tale told roood halle doun lighte stede whiche shoon sonne bright stont court stille ony stoon knyght chambir led anon vnarmed mete sette presentis right richely kept say swerd myrour born anon tour certeyn officer ordeyned therfore vnto canace ring bore solempuly sat tabyl sikr • ly withouten ony fabyl hors bra may reme • yd stont grounde cleuyd none engynys wyndas ne polyue may hit place dryue cause con craft therfore place haue laft til knyght haue taught hem manere widen hym ye shul aftir greet prees swermyd fro gawrin hors stood high brood long wel proporcioned strong right stede lumbardye therwith horsly quyk ye gentil polin courser certis tayl vnto ere nature ne art coude hym amende degre al pepyl wende euermore wonder coude go bra feire al pepyl semyd dyuerse folk diuersly demede meny hedes meny wittis ther mormedyn doth swarm maken skilly aftir hir fantesie rehersynge olde poetrie sayde like pegase hors hadde wyngis forto fle elli grekis hors symon brought grekis vnto destruction men thyse olde gestis rede myn herte quod oon euermore drede trow sum men army therynne shape hem cyte forto wynne right good þ• al suche thing knowe another rowned felow lowe sayde lied rathir lik apparence maad som magik iogelours pleyn festis grete sondry thoughtis thus iangil trete lewd pepyl demen alday comonly thingis maad subtilly konne boundis comprehende demyn gladly badder ende theym wondrid myrour born vp maistir tour men myghte suche thing • se answerde sayde may wel naturelly made composicions aungelis sly reflection sayde rome suche spak alteon vitelon aristotill writin liuys queynte myrours prospectatiuis knowe haue bokis herd othir folk haue wondrid swerd wol perissh thorough euery thing fil speche thelephus kyng achilles queynte spere coude bothe hele dere right suche wyse men may swerd whiche right ye haue self herd speken • ndry hardyng metal speken medicine therwith al whan sholde hardid whiche vnknowe algate speke canaces ryng sayde al suche wonder thing craft ringis herde neuer non saue moyses kyng salamon hadde maner connynge suche art thus seyn pepyl drawen hem apart neuertheles sayde wonder make fern glas yet glas lik as • en fern haue knowe fern therfore secith iangelinge wonder sore wondre som cause thundir ebbe flood gossomer myste al thing til cause wyst thus iangelyn demyn deuyse til kyng gan bord aryse phebus hath lost angil meredional yet ascendyng b • st ryal gentil lioun aldryan whan tartir kyng cambuscan roos bord sat ful hye beforn hym goth lowde mynstralcye tyl cam chambir parementis sownyn dyners instrumentis lik heuen daunsen lusty venus child dere fish lady sat ful hye lokith hem frendly ye nobil kyng set vp trone straunge knyght fet hym ful sone daunce goth canace reuel iolite nat abil adul man deuyse muste haue knowe loue seruise festliche man fresh may shul deuysen suche aray coude telle fourme daunses vncouthe fressh contenaunces therto suche subtil lokyngis drede ielosie mennys preysinges man launcelot ded therfore passe ouer al lustihede say nomore iolynesse lete hem til men sopper hem dresse stiward biddith spicis forto hye • ke wyne al melodye vsshers squiers ben gon spicis wyne comen anon ete drynke whan ende vnto tempyl reson wende seruise haue day nedith reherce aray eche man woot weel kyngis feste hath plente moste leste deyntees mo knowyng aftir sopper goth nobyl kyng se hors bra al route lordis lady hym aboute suche wondryng therof hors bra • ethen grete sege troye men saw suche hors also ne ther suche wondryng tho finally kyng asked knyght vertu courser myght prayde telle hym gouernanuce hors anon gan trippe daunce whan knyght leyde hond reyne sayde sire ther nomore sayne yow list riden ony ye muste trille pyn stont ere whiche shal telle betwix v two ye moot nempne hym place also orto cuntre ye list ryde whan ye come ye list abyde byd hym descende trille another pyn ynne lith effect al gyn wol doun descende al wil place wolde abyde stil theygh al worlde hadde contrary swore shal then drawe ne bore li • bidde hym then goon trille pynne wol vanysshe anon sighte euery maner wight come ayen day nyght yow list clepyn hym aycen • uche gyse shal seyn betwene right sone ride list ther nomore done enfourmed whan kyng knyght hath conceyued wit right maner fourme al thing ful glad blithe nobyl kyng repeyryng vnto reuel beforn bridyl tour yborn kept among iewels leef dere • e hors vanysshed manere sighte ye gete nomore thus lete lust iolite cambuscan lordis festeyng tyl wel nygh day gan sprynge noryce digestiouns sleep gan hem wynke bad hem take kepe muche mete labour wol haue reste galpyng ••• uth hem alle keste sayde tyme lye doun blood domination cherisshed blood nature frend quod thankyn hym galpynge two thre euery wight gan drawe hym rest sleep hem bad took best dremys shul told ful heedes fumosite causith drewe whiche ther charge slepyn til pryme large moste part yf canace ful mesurable wommen fader hadde take leue go reste sone aftir eue list appalled forto ne morow vnfestliche se slept firste sleep wook • uche • oye hir mirrour took bothe ring hir myrrour twenty tyme chaungith colour sleep impression hir mirrour hadde vision̄ wherfore sonne gan vp glide clepid vp maistresse beside sayde lust forto aryse thyse olde wommen ben gladly wyse maistres answerde anon sayde madame whethir wol ye goon thus erly folk alle r • ste wool quod aryse leste lengir slepe walken aboute maistresse clepith wommen greet route vp rysen wel ten twelue vp risith fresh canace selue taried til lust colde hem haue harkened aftir yore sauour passith euer lenger fulsamnes prolixite reson thinkith sholde vnto knotte condescende make hir walkyng end • mydde tre drede whyte chalk canace pleyynge walk ther sat fawoon ouer hed ful hye pitous voys gan crye al wode resowned crye • en hadde self pitouslye bothe wyngis til rede blood ran endlong tre stood euyr one cryde alwey shright bek self pyght ther na tigre cruel beste duellith wode forest wolde haue wept yf wepe coude sorow shriche alwey lowde ther neuer yet man lyue yf coude faucon wel descryue herde suche anothir feirnes wel plumage gentilnes shap al mighte rekened fawoon peregryn semed fremd lond euermore stood swowned lak blood til wel nygh fallen fro tre faire kyngis doughter canace fynger baar queynte ryng thorow whiche vnderstood wel euery thing ony foul may leden seyn coude answere leden agayn hath vnderstonde faucon seyde wel nygh • routhe deyde tre goth ful hastely faucon lokith ful pytously held lappe brood wel wiste faucon muste falle fro twiste whan swowned next lak blood alonge wayte stood til laste spak manere vnto hawke ye shul aftir cause yf forto telle ye furial peyne helle quod canace vnto hauke aboue sorow deth elli loue trow thyse causis two causith gentil herte wo harm reckith speke self vp self wolde wreke whiche preuyth wel ire drede mot encheson cruel dede syn se non wight chace loue god self grace may help west ne est saw neuy • brid best ferde hym self pitously ye sle sorow verily haue gret compassion goddis loue com fro tre adoun kynges doughter trewe verily causis knewe disese yf lay myght wolde amende nyght wi helpe grete god kynde h • rbi shal right ynowe fynde hele • ith hurtis hastely tho shright faucon pitously euer fyl grounde anon lith aswowne ded ony stoon tyl canace hath lappe take vnto tyme gan swowne awake aftir swoun gan brayde right hawkis leden thus sayde pyte rennyth sone gentil herte feling simylitude peynes smerte prouyd alday men may se wel work auctorite gentil herte kidith gentilnesse se wel ye haue distresse compassioun faire canace verry wommanly benignyte nature principlis hath set hope forto fare bet forto obeye herte fre forto make waar whelp chastised lioun right cause conclusioun whyle haue leyser spaas myn harm wil confesse er paas euer whyle sorow tolde othir wepte water wolde til faucon bad hir stille sigh thus said wille bred allas day fostrid roche marbyl gray tenderly thing aylid ne wiste aduersite tyl coude fle ful hye vnder sky tho dwellyd tarcelet faste semed welle al gentilnes al ful treson falsnes wrappid vnder humble chere vnder hue trouthe suche manere vnder plesaunce vnder besy peyne wight wolde haue wend coude feyne depe greyn died colour right serpent hidith hym vnder flouris til may see tyme forto byte right god loue ipocryte doth • rymoyns obeysauncis kepith semblaunce al obseruauncis • wneth vnto gentilnesse loue tombe al feyr aboue vnder corp suche ye woot suche ipocrit bothe cold hoot wyse seruid entent saue fende noman wist ment til longe hadde wept compleyned meny yeer seruise vnto feyned til herte pitous nyce al innocent crowned malice ferd deth thoughte vp othis suerte graunte hym loue vp condicion euermo myn honour renoun saued bothe pryue apert seyn aftir desert yaf hym al herte al thought god woot wyse nought toke herte change myn ay soth said goon seth many aday trewe wight theef thinke whan saw thing fer agon grauntid hym loue suche agyse haue sayd aboue yeue hym trewe herte fre swoor yaf herte anon tigre ful doubilnesse fil knee gret humblenesse high reuerence chere lik gentil louer manere rauysshed semed ioye neuer troylus ne paris troye iason certis ne non man syn lameth alder first began louen two writen folk beforn ne neuer sith first man born ony womman neuer wyse payntid • e chere poynt deuyce wel wordis contenaunce loued hym obeisaunce trowthe demed hert • ony thing hym smert al neuer lite wiste thoughte herde deth herte twiste shortly ferforth thing went wil willis instrument sey wil obeyed wil alle thing aftir reson fyl kepyng boundis worship euer ne neuer hadde thing leef ne leuer hym god woot ne neuer shal nomo lastid lenger yeer two • upposid hym thing good finally thus laste stood fortune wolde must twynne place whiche inne woo questioun make discripcion thing dar telle boldly knowe peyne deth therby suche harm mette ne mighte leue day took leue sorowfully eke wende verily hadde felt muche sorow herde hym speke saw hewe neuerthelesse thoughte trewe eke repayre sholde agayn ynne litil whyle soth sayn reson wolde eke moste go honour ofte fallith made vertu necessite took wel syn nedes moste best myghte hid fro hym sorow took hym hond se •• iohn borow sayde thus lo youris al bothe suche haue shal answerde nedith reherce say bet wers whan hath al sayd hath doon therfore behoueth hym haue long spoon shal ete fende thus herde say acte laste muste forth way forth fleith til com hym leste cam hym purpos reste trow hadde text mynde al thing repeyrith kynde gladith hym self thus sey men gesse men loue propir kynde newefangilnesse briddis doon men cagis fede thou nyght day take hem hede strawe cage feyre softe silk yeue hem suger hony bred mylk yet right anon dore vp foot spurneth doun cup wode wol wormes ete newfangil ben mete loue noueltees proper kynde gentilnesse blood may hym bynde ferde tarcellet allas day though gentil born fresh gay goodly forto se humble fre saw vp tyme kyte fle sodenly louyd kyte al loue clene fro go hath trouthe falsid wyse thus hath kyte loue seruise lorn withoute remedy word faucon gan cry swouned eft canaces arm greet sorow hawkis harm canace alle woman made nyste myghte faucon glade canace hoom berith lappe softly plasteris gan wrappe bek hadde hurt selue canace herbis delue grounde make plastris newe herbis precious fyne hewe hele hauke fro day nyght doth besines al myght beddis hed made mewe couered veluettis blewe signe trouthe woman seen al withoute mewe peyntid green whiche pryntid al thyse false • ulis thyse tidi •• tarcellis owlis right dispyt peyntid besyde pie theym forto crye chyde thus lete canace hauk kepyng wol nomore speke ryng til come efte purpoos forto sayn faucon gat loue agayn repentyng story tellith v mediacion cambalus kyngis sone whiche zou tolde hen forth wol processe holde speken auenturis batayllis yet neuer herd grete meruayllis first wol telle cambuscan tyme many cyte wan aftir wyl speke algarsif wan theodora wif ful ofte greet peril ne hadde holpyn hors bra aftir wol speke camballo faught listis bretheren two canace myghte wynn • lefte wol ayen begynne appollo whirlith vp chare high til god mercurius sligh endith squy • ri tale begynneth marchan̄tis prolog wepynge waylinge care sorow knowe nough bothe euen ek morow quod marchaunt doth oth • r mo weddid trow wel woot fareth • e haue wyf worste may though feend coupled • ere wolde hym ouermacche dar wel swere sholde reherce special high malice shrewe al ther long large difference betwix grisildis grete pacience wyf passing cruelte vnbounde also mot wolde neuer efte come snare weddid men lyue sorow care say wol shal fynde say soth saint thomas inde part say al god shilde sholde fal good sir oost haue weddid thyse monethis two nomore parde yet trow hath al lif weddid though men wolde hym ryf herte ne coude maner telle muche sorow coude telle wyues cursidnes quod ofte marchaunt god blisse syn ye mykil konne • f art ful h • rtely pray tel v part gladly quod myn owen sore sory herte telle may nomore ¶here endith prolog ¶and begynneth marchauntis tale somtyme ther duellynge lumbardye worthy knyght born pauy whiche liuyd gret prosperyte lx yeer wyfl • e man folowyd bodily delyt woman hool appetyt doon thyse folis ben seculer whan passid lx yeer holinesse dotage say suche gret corage hadde knyght weddid man day nyght doth al aspye myghte weddid prayyng lord grauntinge myghte onys knowe blisful lif betwix husbonde wyf forto lyue vnder holy bond whiche god first man wom̄an bond non lif sayde worth bene wedlok esy clene worlde paradise thus sayde olde knyght wyse certeinly soth god kyng take wyf glorious thing namely whan man old hoor wyf fruyt tresoor sholde take yong wyf feir whiche myghte engendre hym heir lede lif ioye solace thyse bachelers syngen allas fynde ony aduersite loue whiche childis vanite trewly sit wel bachelers haue ofte peyne woo brotil ground bilde brotilnesse fynde freelte whan wene sikirnesse lyue brid best liberte vnder non areest weddid man astaat liueth lif blisful ordinate vnder yok mariage bounde wel may herte ioye blisse habound • buxum wyf trewe tentif kepe hym seek hool make weel woo wol nat hym forsake nat wery hym loue serue though lye bedrede til sterue yet clerkis sayn whiche theophraste tho fors theygh theophraste doth lye ne take wyf quod husbondrye forto spare housholde thyn expence trewe seruaunt doth diligence thy good kepe doth thy self wyf wol clayme half part al lif yf thow seek god saue thy verey frendis trewe knaue wol kepe bet waytith ay aftir thy good hath meny day take kepe suche vanyte fy theophraste herken wyf goddis ziste verily al maner zistis hardely londis rentis pasturis com̄une othir yeftis meuable fortune passen shadow wal drede yf playnly speke shal wyf wil laste thy hous endure wel lenger liste ꝑauenture mariage ful greet sacrament hath wyf shent liuyth helples al desolat speke folk seculer astat herken say nought womman mannys help wrought high god whan hadde adam makid saw hym allone bely nakid god grete goodnesse sayde let v make help man lik hym self made eue may ye se preue wyf mannys help comfort paradyse terrestre disport buxum vertuous muste nedis liue vnite flessh blood gesse one herte wyl distresse wyf saynte mary benedicite mighte aman haue ony aduersite hath wyf certis sey blisse betwix hem twey ther may tunge telle herte thynke poure helpith hym swynke kepith good wastith neuer deel al husbond lust likith weel saith onys nay whan saith ye saith al redy sire saith blisful ordre wedlok precious thou art mery • ek ioyous comendid approued eke euery man holdeth hym worth leek vp bare knee oughte al lif thankin god hym sent wyf elli praye g • hym forto sende wyf laste liues ende lif set sik • cnesse may disceyued gesse worke aftir wyues rede may boldely bere vp hede trewe therto eke wyse whiche yf thou wolt worche wyse alwey woman wol rede lo iacob thyse clerkis rede good counsel moder rebek bond kiddi • skyn aboute nek whiche fadris benyson wan lo iudith story wel telle wyse counsel goddis pepil kepte slew hym olofernes whyle slepte lo abigayl good counsel saued husbonde nabal whan shulde haue slayn loke hester also good counsel deliuered •• wo pepyl god made • ardoche assuere enhaunced forto ther thing gre superlatif saith senek aboue humble wyf suffre thy wyuys tunge caton bit shal comaunde thou shalt suffre yet wylle obeye curtesie wyf keper thy husbondrye wel may seek man bewayle wepe wyf hous kepe warne thou wysely wilt wirche loue wel thy wyf crist loueth chirche thou louest thy self thou louest thy wyf noman hatith flessh lif suffrith therfore bidde cherisshe thy wyf thou woman twenty yeer age bene straw greet forage eke thyse olde wydowes god woot conne mykyl craft wadi boot mykyl harm hem list hem sholde neuer lyue rest sondry scolis makith subtil clerkis woman many scole half clerk certeinly yong thing may men gye right man hondis warm wexe plye therfore say pleynly clause wol non olde wyf haue cause yf yf hadde suche myschaunce coude haue plesaunce sholde lede lif avontrye streight deuel whan dye ne child sholde non getyn yet hadde leuyr houndis hadde etyn myn heritage shulde falle straunge hond thus telle al doute woot cause men sholde wedde ferthermore woot spekith meny men mariage woot nomore doth page whiche causis men sholde take wyf yf may chast wyf take hym wyf greet deuocion cause lefful procreacion childryn honour god aboue paramour ne loue sholde lecherye eschue yelde dette newe eche man sholde helpe othir myschief sustir shal brothir lyue chastite ful heuenly sire leue god bethankid dar make auaunt fele lymys stark sufficiaunt al aman behoueth strong ynough ride goo though hoor fare doth tre blesmeth tre grene blosmed tre neyther drye ne ded fele hoor myn hed herte lymes ay grene laurer thorow yeer sene sithnys ye haue herd al myn entent pray wyl ye assent diuers men diuersly hym tolde mariage meny ensamplis olde som blamed preysid certeyn laste shortly forto seyn alday falleth altercacion betwix frendis disputacion ther fyl strif betwix bretheren two whiche clepid placebo placebo sayde ianuary brother telle tale non ful litil nede ye lord dere counsel ax • ony ye ful sapience ne likith high prudence weyue fro word salamon word • yde v euerichon worke al thing counfel thus sayde shalt thou repente though salamon spak suche word myn owen dere brother lord wyssely god soule brynge reste holde owen counsel best brother myn take motyf haue courtman al lyf yet god woot though vnworthy haue stonde ful gret degre aboute lordis ful gret astaat yet hadde neuer non hem debaat neuer contraried hem trewly woot wel lord seith holde ferm stabil say othir thing semblable ful gret fool ony counselour seruith lord high honour dar presume onys thynke counsel sholde passe lordis wit nay lordis folis fay ye haue self spoken day high sentence holy wel consente conferme eueridel wordis al oppinion god ther noman toun ne ytaille coude better haue sayd crist holdith hym ful wel payd trewly high corage ony man stept age take yong wyf • ader kyn herte hongith vp ioly pyn doth mater lest finally holde best iustimis ay sat ful stille playde right wyse placebo sayde brother myn quod pacient pray syn ye haue sayd herde thing sayde farid hadde stert slep • til hir masidnes abreyde grisilde quod god v deyde thow art wyf non haue ne neuer hadde god soule saue thy doughter whiche thou hast supposid wyf othir feithfully shal myn heir haue disposid thou baar hym thy body ful trewly boleyne haue kept hem priuely take hem ayeen maist thou nat sey thou hast lorn none thy childryn twey folk othir wyse haue sayd warne hem wel haue dede malice ne cruelte forto assay thy womanhede nat sle childryn god forbede forto kepe hem priuely stille til thy purpos knew al thy wylle herde swonnyng doun fallith pitous ioye aftir swonnyng bothe yonge childryn callith army ful petously wepynge enbraced hem tenderly kissinge ful lik amodir salt teris badith bothe visage eris whiche pitous thing se swonn • nge pitous vois syn mankynde fair part thy werk thou maad first lik thyn owen merk semyth ye haue gret charite toward mankynde mighte ye suche menys make destroien suche menes good annoien woot wel clerkis wol say ful • ute plesaunce anon aftir dyner gonne daun •• song also saue dorigene alone whiche made alwey compleynt hir mone ne saw hym • daunce go husbond loue also natheles must tyme abyde good hope lete sorowis slyde vp daunce among men daunsid squier befor dorigene fressher iolier assay dome monthe may singith daunsith passing ony • syn worlde began therwith yf men sholde hym discryue beste faryng men lyue yong strong vertuous wyse wel belouyd holdyn gret price shortly yf soth telle shall vnwytyng dorigene al lusty squier seruaunt venus whiche clepid aurelius louyd best ony creature two yeer auenture neuer durste telle greuaunce withoute cup drank al penaunce despeyr • thing durste sey saue songis somdele wolde wrey general compleynynge said louyd belouyd thing suche mater made many layis yonge • olk kepyn obseruaunci • may weel ben lokid face suche wyse • n axen grace thing wiste entent natheles happid then went cause neyghebour man worship honour hadde knowen hym tymes yore fallen speche purpos drew aurilius whan saw tyme said thus madame quod god worlde made wiste mighte herte glade wolde day arueragus went ouer se aurelius gone sholde neuer come ayeen wel woot seruise veyn guerdom brestyng myn herte madame rewe peynys smerte foot god wolde begraue wisly god sowle saue ne haue leyser seye haue mercy swete ye wol deye gan loke vp aurelius wil quod say ye thus neuer yet quod wist ye ment ne neuer vnderstode entent god yaf soule lif ne shal neuer vntrew wif word ne werk fer haue wyt wil knyt take fynal answer aftir pley thus said aurely said high god aboue yet wol whyle sekyn diuinite hid heuene priuely algate b • ent worlde shal cecily answerde boldly men mighte drede wel skilfully lif like myn owen dere brother liuynge non oth • r bettir lif place neuer shal prechinge eue gonne fro turmentours forto reue fro maxime fro folk echone fals feith trowe god allone cecily cam woxe nyght preestis hem cristned alle fere afterward whan day woren light cecily sayde synne recke beried though soulis goon blakeberied certis many predicacion sowneth ofte tyme euyentencion plesaunce folk flaterye ben auauncid ypocrisie som veynglory som hate dar whyle debate wol displesauncis thus spit venym vnder hewe holynes seme holy trewe shortly myn entent wol deuyse preche thing couetyse therfore teme yet euer radix oīm malo rum est cupiditas thus gan preche wyse suche spoke befo • n̄ many grisly oth haue sworn̄ cristis blissid body rente deth shal ded yf may hym hente haue goon fully myle right wolde haue goon ouer style old poure man hem mette olde man full mekely hem grette sayde thus lordingis god se proudest thyse riotours thre answerde charl hard grace art thow al forwrappid saue thy face l • uyst thou longe gret age olde man gan loke visage sayde thus fynde man though walke ynde neyther cyte ne village wol chaunge yonthe myn age therfore muste haue myn age still longe tyme goddis ne deth allas wol haue lyf thus walke lik recheles caytiff grounde whiche modris gate knocke staf erly late say leue modir lete yn lo vanyssh flesh blood skyn allas whan shal honys reste modir wolde chaunge cheste chambir longe tyme hath ye heir clout wrappe ynne yet wol grace whiche ful paal wrecchid face seris curtesie speke olde man vilony trespasse othir word dede ye may self holy writ rede ayenst olde man hore vp heed ye sholde ryse wherfore rede ne doth non olde man harm nomore ye wolde men dide age yf ye sholde longe abyde god wher ye go ryde muste go thyder haue nay olde chorle god thou shalt seyde othir hasardour anon thou partist lightly seynt iohn thou spakist right treitour deth contre al frendis sleth haue trouthe thou art aspye tel thou shalt dye god holy sacrement shortly thou art one assent sle v yonge folk thou fals theef seris yf leef thyse riotouris ran til cam tre found floreyns fyn golde coyned rounde wel nye echte busshellis hem thoughte lengir aftir deth soughte ech theym glad sighte floreyns fair brighte doun sat precyous
